Home Collector’s Centre Ira Welcome Deck
Ira Welcome Deck
Printed in December 2018, the Ira Welcome Deck is provided to local game stores free of charge. There are 12 cards in the set, making up a total 32 card deck for new players to learn the basics of Flesh and Blood. These come with a simple rules insert, and were included as part of our retailer appreciation kit.

The Ira Welcome Deck is featured in the Flesh and Blood learn to play video.

Print Run	Date Printed	Printed In	Languages	Size of Print Run
First	December 2018	Belgium	English	45,000 decks
Second	December 2020	Belgium	English	56,000 decks
Third	October 2021	Belgium	English	100,000 decks
Fourth	June 2022	Belgium	English, French, German, Italian, Spanish	66,000 decks
Fifth	July 2023	Japan	English	TBA
Sixth	TBC	Japan	Japanese	TBA
Code	Card Name	Printing Technique	Notes
IRA001-P	Ira Crimson Haze	Normal	The December 2018 version of Ira was printed without the “young” sub-type. This was added later when she released in Crucible of War, in order to make her legal for the Blitz format.
The 2020 version had the “young” sub-type added and the set code updated to CRU046.
IRA002-P	Edge of Autumn	Normal	The December 2018 version of Edge of Autumn has gold embellishments on the card frame, something that would become reserved for legendary equipment and weapons.
The 2020 reprint had the set code updated to CRU050 and the gold embellishments removed.
IRA003-P	Whirling Mist Blossom	Normal	The 2020 reprint had the set code updated to CRU074.
IRA004-P	Salt the Wound	Normal	The 2020 reprint had the set code updated to CRU073.
IRA005-P	Bittering Thorns	Normal	The 2020 reprint had the set code updated to CRU072.
IRA006-P	Torrent of Tempo	Normal	The 2020 reprint had the set code updated to CRU069.
IRA007-P	Flying Kick	Normal	The 2020 reprint had the set code updated to CRU063.
IRA008-P	Head Jab	Normal	The 2020 reprint no longer has the ‘Pop art’ and had the set code updated to WTR100.
IRA009-P	Scar for a Scar	Normal	The 2020 reprint had a non-functional syntax update and the set code updated to WTR191.
IRA010-P	Brutal Assault	Normal	The 2020 reprint had the set code updated to CRU194.
IRA011-P	Lunging Press	Normal	The 2020 reprint had the set code updated to CRU186.
IRA012-P	Springboard Somersault	Normal	The 2020 reprint had the set code updated to CRU

Home Collector’s Centre Welcome to Rathe
Welcome to Rathe
Welcome to Rathe is the first booster and hero deck set for Flesh and Blood. It released October 11th, 2019 in local game stores across the USA, Australia, and New Zealand.

Welcome to Rathe introduced four heroes:

Bravo, Showstopper, a flamboyant Guardian
Dorinthea Ironsong, a virtuous Warrior
Katsu, the Wanderer, a Ninja on a journey to discover himself
Rhinar, Reckless Rampage, an apex predator Brute
The Welcome to Rathe booster set contains a total of 226 cards, with the following configuration and estimated rarity breakdown:

1 Fabled (1 per ??? packs)
5 Legendary (1 per 96 packs)
10 Majestic (1 per 12 packs)
15 Super Rares (1 per 6 packs)
48 Rares (1.75 per pack)
132 Commons (12 per pack)
15 Tokens (1 per pack)
Premium Foil (1 per pack, with Alpha Print containing 1 Cold Foil every 24 packs)
Each hero was available as a pre-constructed Hero Deck, playable out of the box. Each Hero Deck contained a cohesive 60 card deck + hero card, weapon, equipment set, and rule book.

Print Run	Date Printed	Printed In	Languages	Out of Print	Size of Print Run
Alpha Edition (Booster)	August 2019	Belgium	English	Yes	16,700 displays
Unlimited Edition (Booster)	From September 2020	Belgium & Japan	English	Yes	248,000 displays
Hero Decks	August 2019	Belgium	English	Yes	10,000 Bravo decks
10,000 Dorinthea decks
10,000 Katsu decks
10,000 Rhinar decks

Home Collector’s Centre Arcane Rising
Arcane Rising
Arcane Rising is the second booster set for Flesh and Blood. It released March 27th, 2020 in local game stores across the USA, Australia, New Zealand, Taiwan, and Malaysia.

Arcane Rising introduced four heroes:

Dash, Inventor Extraordinaire, a brilliant Mechanologist
Azalea, Ace in the Hole, a cool-headed Ranger
Viserai, Rune Blood, the terrifying Runeblade
Kano, Dracai of Aether, the Wizard with a flare for the dramatic
The Arcane Rising booster set contains a total of 219 cards, with the following configuration and estimated rarity breakdown:

1 Fabled (1 per ??? packs)
5 Legendary (1 per 96 packs)
10 Majestic (1 per 12 packs)
15 Super Rares (1 per 6 packs)
48 Rares (1.75 per pack)
126 Commons (12 per pack)
14 Tokens (1 per pack)
Premium Foil (1 per pack, with First Edition containing 1 Cold Foil every 24 packs)
Print Run	Date Printed	Printed In	Languages	Out of Print	Size of Print Run
First Edition	December 2019	Belgium	English	Yes	16,700 displays
Unlimited Edition	From October 2020	Belgium	English	Yes	179,000 displays

Home Collector’s Centre Crucible of War
Crucible of War
Crucible of War is the third booster set for Flesh and Blood, also being the first supplementary booster set. It released on August 28th, 2020 in local game stores across the USA, Australia, New Zealand, Taiwan, and Malaysia.

A supplementary booster set is designed specifically to enhance and expand constructed play and is not designed for booster draft play.

Crucible of War introduced six new young heroes:

Kayo, Berserker Runt, a Brute that packs a punch
Benji, the Piercing Wind, a nimble Ninja
Kassai, Cintari Sellsword, a Warrior seeking spoils of war
Shiyana, Diamond Gemini, a diplomatic Shapeshifter
Data Doll MKII, an artificial Mechnologist
Kavdaen, Trader of Skins, a Merchant where no deal is off the table
The Crucible of War booster set contains a total of 198 cards, with the following configuration and estimated rarity breakdown:

1 Fabled (1 per ??? packs)
2 Legendary (1 per 240 packs)
36 Majestic (1 per 4 packs)
56 Rare (1.75 per pack)
103 Common (7 per pack)
Premium Foil (1 per pack, with First Edition containing 1 Cold Foil every 22 packs)
Print Run	Date Printed	Printed In	Languages	Out of Print	Size of Print Run
First Edition	June 2020, August 2020	Belgium	English	Yes	37,500 displays
Unlimited Edition	From June 2021	Japan	English	Yes	125,000 displays

Home Collector’s Centre Monarch
Monarch
Monarch is the fourth booster set for Flesh and Blood. It released May 7th, 2021 in local game stores across the USA, United Kingdom, Australia, New Zealand, Taiwan, Malaysia and most European countries.

Monarch introduced four heroes:

Ser Boltyn, Breaker of Dawn, a valiant Light Warrior
Prism, Sculptor of Arc Light, an intelligent Light Illusionist
Levia, Shadowborn Abomination, a bloodthirsty Shadow Brute
Chane, Bound by Shadow, a Shadow Runeblade consumed by darkness
The Monarch booster set contains a total of 307 cards, with the following configuration and estimated rarity breakdown:

1 Fabled (1 per ??? packs)
6 Legendary (1 per 96 packs)
31 Majestic (1 per 4 packs)
79 Rares (1.75 per pack)
172 Commons (12 per pack)
18 Tokens (1 per pack)
Premium Foil (1 per pack, with First Edition containing 1 Cold Foil every 22 packs)
Each hero was available as a pre-constructed Blitz Deck, playable out of the box. Each Hero Deck contained a cohesive 40 card deck + hero card, weapon, equipment set, tokens if required.

Print Run	Date Printed	Printed In	Languages	Out of Print	Size of Print Run
First Edition (Booster)	January 2021	Belgium	English	Yes	125,000 displays
Unlimited Edition (Booster)	From April 2021	Belgium & Japan	English	Yes	181,000 displays
Blitz Decks	From March 2021	Belgium & Japan	English	Yes	~

Home Collector’s Centre Tales of Aria
Tales of Aria
Tales of Aria is the fifth booster set for Flesh and Blood. It was released on September 24th, 2021 in local game stores across the USA, Europe, and Asia-Pacific region.

Tales of Aria introduced three heroes:

Oldhim, Grandfather of Eternity, an Elemental Guardian
Lexi, Live Wire, an Elemental Ranger
Briar, Warden of Thorns, an Elemental Runeblade
The Tales of Aria booster set contains a total of 238 cards, with the following configuration and estimated rarity breakdown:

1 Fabled (1 per ??? packs)
6 Legendary (1 per 88 packs)
27 Majestic (1 per 4 packs)
54 Rares (1.75 per pack)
136 Commons (12 per pack)
14 Tokens (1 per pack)
Premium Foil (1 per pack, with First Edition also containing 1 Cold Foil every 20 packs)
Each hero was available as a pre-constructed Blitz Deck, playable out of the box. Each Hero Deck contained a cohesive 40 card deck + hero card, weapon, equipment set, and tokens if required.

Print Run	Date Printed	Printed In	Languages	Out of Print	Size of Print Run
First Edition (Booster)	June 2021	Belgium	English	Yes	208,000 displays
Unlimited Edition (Booster)	From July 2021	Belgium & Japan	English	Yes	76,000 displays
Blitz Decks	From July 2021	Belgium & Japan	English	Yes	~

Home Collector’s Centre Everfest
Everfest
Everfest is the Sixth booster set for Flesh and Blood, also being the second supplementary booster set. It released on February 4th, 2022 in local game stores across the USA, Europe, and Asia-Pacific region.

Everfest introduced four new heroes:

The one and only Bravo, Star of the Show!
Valda Brightaxe, a Guardian with no patience for cocky patrons
Ready your silver for Genis Wotchuneed, a roaming Merchant
The Elemental Wizard Iyslander, mystery of the Bleak Expanse
The Everfest booster set contains a total of 198 cards, with the following configuration and estimated rarity breakdown:

1 Fabled (1 per ??? packs)
3 Legendary (1 per 160 packs)
45 Majestic (1 per 4 packs, with a chance at a Carnival themed Majestic at 1 per 26 packs)
61 Rares (1.65 per pack)
88 Commons (7 per pack)
Rainbow Foil (1 per pack)
Cold Foil (1 per 16 packs)
Print Run	Date Printed	Printed In	Languages	Out of Print	Size of Print Run
First Edition (Booster)	October 2021	Belgium	English	Yes	229,000 displays
Unlimited Edition (Booster)	October 2021	Belgium	English	Yes	40 displays

Home Collector’s Centre History Pack 1
History Pack 1
History Pack 1 contains many of the key cards from the first year of Flesh and Blood (Welcome to Rathe, Arcane Rising, and Crucible of War), curated into a single white-border set.

A special print run of Black Label product has been translated into German, French, Spanish, and Italian. The Black Label printing features black border cards and has special cold foils unique to the product.

The English edition released on May 6th, 2022 in local games stores across USA, Europe, and Asia-Pacific. The Black Label foreign language products released on July 1st, 2022 in local games stores across Europe.

History Pack 1 booster set contains a total of 427* cards, with the following configuration and estimated rarity breakdown:

9 Legendary (1 per 82 packs)
62 Majestic (1 per 3.15 packs)
118 Rares (1.65 per pack)
208 Commons (7 per pack)
*3 Fabled (1 per ???) – only features in Black Label product
*8 Marvel (1 per ???) – only featured in Black Label product
History Pack 1 Blitz decks released February 24, 2023 throughout Europe in local languages; German, Spanish, Italian and French. English edition release is April 7, 2023.

Ready-to-play out of the box, History Pack 1 Blitz Decks are crafted as an ideal product for kitchen table gaming, and features 6 iconic ready-to-play characters from the history of Flesh and Blood.

Print Run	Date Printed	Printed In	Languages	Out of Print	Size of Print Run
Booster (White Border)	From October 2021	Japan	English	Yes	TBA
Booster (Black Label)	January 2022	Belgium	German, Spanish, Italian, French	Yes	French – 13,000 displays
German – 13,000 displays
Italian – 6,000 displays
Spanish – 13,000 displays
Blitz Decks	From October 2022	Belgium	English, German, Spanish, Italian, French	Yes	TBD

Home Collector’s Centre Uprising
Uprising
Uprising is the seventh booster set for Flesh and Blood TCG. It was released on June 24th, 2022 in local game stores across the Europe, and Asia-Pacific region, then released on July 1st, 2022 in the USA.

The Uprising booster set introduces an incredible new marvel rarity.

Uprising introduced three heroes:

Dromai, Ash Artist, an Imperial Draconic Illusionist able to conjure the legendary dragons of Volcor out of aether and ash.
Fai, Rising Rebellion, a hot-headed Draconic Ninja who spearheads the Uprising against the draconian oppression of the Imperials.
Iyslander, Stormbind, an Elemental Wizard who is in search of answers to painful questions seared deep within her mind.
The Uprising booster set contains a total of 226 cards, with the following configuration and estimated rarity breakdown:

1 Fabled (1 per ??? packs)
6 Legendary (Rainbow Foil – 1 per 80 packs), (Cold Foil – 1 per 220 packs)
27 Majestic (1 per 4 packs)
51 Rares (1.75 per pack)
125 Commons (11 per pack)
16 Tokens (1.75 tokens per pack)
Premium Foil (1 per pack)
Cold Foil (1 per 24 packs)
Marvel (1 per ??? packs)
Dromai and Fai are available as pre-constructed Blitz Decks, playable out of the box. Each Hero Deck contained a cohesive 40-card deck + hero card, weapon, equipment set, and tokens if required.

Print Run	Date Printed	Printed In	Languages	Out of Print	Size of Print Run
Booster	From March 2022	Belgium	English	Yes	212,000 displays
Blitz Decks	From April 2022	Belgium	English	Yes	~

Home Collector’s Centre Dynasty
Dynasty
Dynasty is an expansion booster set, and the eighth booster release for Flesh and Blood TCG. It was released on November 11th, 2022 in local game stores across the USA, Europe, and the Asia-Pacific region.

Dynasty continues the story from Uprising and supports all main classes in Flesh and Blood, as well as introduces the long awaited Assassin class.

Dynasty introduces 3 new heroes:

Emperor, Dracai of Aesir – a Royal Draconic Warrior Wizard that sits upon the Imperial throne of Volcor.
Yoji, Royal Protector – an Imperial Guardian tasked with protecting the Emperor.
Arakni, Huntsman – The cunning Assassin tasked with executing the Emperor.
Dynasty contains a total of 246 cards, with the following configuration and estimated rarity breakdown:

1 Fabled (1 per ??? packs)
14 Marvel (1 per ??? packs)
5 Legendary (Rainbow Foil – 1:88 packs // Cold Foil – 1:280 packs)
51 Majestic (1:4 packs)
81 Rares (1.75 per pack)
109 Commons (7 per pack)
Cold Foil (1:24 packs)
Premium Foil (1 per pack)
Print Run	Date Printed	Printed In	Languages	Out of Print	Size of Print Run
Booster	From August 2022	Belgium	English	Yes	168,000 displays

Home Collector’s Centre History Pack 2
History Pack 2
History Pack 2 contains many of the key cards from the second year of Flesh and Blood, curated into a single black border set for French, German, Italian, and Spanish speaking fans. It released in the supported countries on February 24, 2023.

To celebrate the release of History Pack 2 in localized European languages for the first time, we have crafted a limited edition Black Label version of History Pack 2 that includes the three Fabled cards from this era! Subsequent printings of History Pack 2 will be printed in white border.

History Pack 2 released February 24, 2023.

History Pack 2 booster set contains a total of 536 cards, with the following configuration and estimated rarity breakdown:

10 cards per pack. 36 packs per display. 4 displays per case.

14 Legendary (1 per 60 packs)
78 Majestic (1 per 3.5 packs)
140 Rares (1.7 per pack)
301 Commons (7 per pack)
3 Fabled (1 per ???)
Print Run	Date Printed	Printed In	Languages	Out of Print	Size of Print Run

Home Collector’s Centre Outsiders
Outsiders
Outsiders is the ninth booster set for Flesh and Blood TCG. It was released on March 24th, 2023 in local game stores across the world. Outsiders is the first Flesh and Blood booster set to release in local languages around the world along side the English print.

Languages: English, German, French, Italian, Spanish

Outsiders introduced three new hero’s while also revisiting three fan favorites:

Uzuri, Switchblade
Riptide, Lurker of the Deep
Arakni, Solitary Confinement
Katsu, the Wanderer
Azalea, Ace in the Hole
Benji, the Piercing Wind
The Outisders booster set contains a total of 239 cards, with the following configuration and estimated rarity breakdown:

1 Fabled (1 per ??? packs)
5 Legendary (Rainbow Foil – 1:70 packs / Cold Foil – 1:264 packs)
31 Majestic (1 per 5 packs)
51 Rares (1.75 per pack)
128 Commons (11 per pack)
20 Tokens (1.75 tokens per pack)
Premium Foil (1 per pack)
Cold Foil (1 per 24 packs)
3 Marvels (1 per ??? packs)
All hero’s featured in Outsiders also have their own Blitz decks. Each Hero Deck contained a cohesive 40-card deck + hero card, weapon, equipment set, and tokens if required perfect for kitchen table gaming and learning how to play Flesh and Blood!

Print Run	Date Printed	Printed In	Languages	Out of Print	Size of Print Run
Booster	From December 2022	Belgium, Japan	English, German, French, Italian, Spanish	Yes	169,000 displays
Blitz Decks	From December 2022	Belgium	English, German, French, Italian, Spanish	Yes	~

Home Collector’s Centre Dusk till Dawn
Dusk till Dawn
Dusk till Dawn is an expansion booster set. It is Flesh and Blood TCGs tenth set release.

Worldwide Release date: July 14th, 2023
Languages: English, German, French, Italian, and Spanish
As the tenth milestone set, Dusk till Dawn includes hand drawn artist sketch serialized cards to celebrate the first Light and Shadow Living Legend hero’s; Prism, Sculptor of Arc Light and Chane, Bound by Shadow.

Dusk till Dawn expands on constructed formats and features the following hero’s:

Prism, Awakener of Sol
Vynnset, Iron Maiden
Ser Boltyn, Breaker of Dawn
Levia, Shadowborn Abomination

Home Collector’s Centre Bright Lights
Bright Lights
Bright Lights is a core booster set. It is Flesh and Blood TCGs eleventh booster set release.

Worldwide Release date: October 6th, 2023
Languages: English, German, French, Italian, and Spanish
Bright Lights takes Flesh and Blood game play to new frontiers of innovation, with the first ever equipment that start the game in the deck. It also introduces a new and simple way to play Flesh and Blood; 3-Pack Crack, Shuffle, Play.

Bright Lights introduces the Expansion Slot, a new feature starting with Bright Lights that offers new content to support a range of heroes outside those featured in the product itself. There are 15 Expansion cards in Bright Lights that feature approximately 1 per 15 packs.

Bright Lights introduces 3 new hero’s, one of which is a newly imagined version of fan favorite; Dash!

Dash I/O
Maxx ‘The Hype’ Nitro
Teklovossen, Esteemed Magnate
The Bright Lights booster set contains a total of 251 cards, with the following configuration and estimated rarity breakdown:

1 Fabled (1 per ??? packs)
7 Legendary (1 per 70 packs)
46 Majestic (1 per 4 packs)
56 Rare (1.68 per pack)
129 Common (11 per pack)
12 Token (1.8~ per pack)
Premium Foil (1 per pack)
Cold Foil (1 per 24 packs)
9 Marvels (1 per ??? packs)

Home Collector’s Centre Heavy Hitters
Heavy Hitters
Heavy Hitters is a core booster set. It is Flesh and Blood TCGs twelfth booster set release.

Worldwide Release date: February 2, 2024
Languages: English, German, French, Italian, and Spanish
Heavy Hitters brings the biggest, strongest, hardest hitting fun to Flesh and Blood gaming tables yet! Featuring six heroes across Brute, Guardian, and Warrior classes, crossover hybrid cards, and more weapons and equipment than any draftable set before, the number of options for how you bring your fight to the arena are huge!

The Heavy Hitters Deathmatch Arena contestants are:

Kayo, Armed and Dangerous
Rhinar, Reckless Rampage
Betsy, Skin in the Game
Victor Goldmane, High and Mighty
Kassai of the Golden Sands
Olympia, Prized Fighter
Heavy Hitters booster set contains a total of 256 cards, with the following configuration and estimated rarity breakdown:

40* Majestic (1 per 4 packs)
66** Rare (1.83 per pack)
128 Common (11 per pack)
15 Token (1.85 per pack)
Premium Foil (1 per pack)
5 Legendary (1 per 96 packs)
31 Majestic (1 per 18 packs)
51 Rare (5 per 24 packs)
92 Common (18 per 24 packs)
33 Cold Foil (1 per 24 packs)
1 Fabled
5 Legendary
3 Majestic
7 Rare
17 Common
10 Marvels (1 per 192 packs)
*10 Majestics are Expansion content to support hero’s and classes that are not feature in the core product.
**High Riser is upshifted from Token to Rare when in Cold Foil
All hero’s featured in Heavy Hitters also have their own Blitz decks. Each Hero Deck contained a cohesive 40-card deck + hero card, weapon, equipment set, and tokens if required perfect for kitchen table gaming and learning how to play Flesh and Blood!

Print Run	Date Printed	Printed In	Languages	Out of Print	Size of Print Run
Booster	November 2023	Belgium, Japan	EN / DE / FR / IT / SP	Yes	TBA
Booster	June 2024	Japan	JP	Yes	TBA
Blitz Deck	From November 2023	Belgium	EN	Yes	TBA

Home Collector’s Centre Part the Mistveil
Part the Mistveil
Part the Mistveil is a core booster set. It is Flesh and Blood TCGs thirteenth booster set release.

Worldwide Release date: May 31st, 2024
Languages: English, Japanese, German, French, Italian, and Spanish
Part the Mistveil features breath-taking Marvel heroes and traditional Japanese illustration cards, a diverse range of support cards within the Expansion Slot, and is the first Flesh and Blood booster set to be released in Japanese language!

Venture into the cloaked valleys of Misteria to uncover ancient truths and traditions that will reshape your mind, body, and soul! Part the Mistveil features three new heroes across Assassin, Ninja, and Illusionist classes, as well as the incredible new Mystic talent.

Seduce your enemies with the Mystic Assassin; Nuu, Alluring Desire
Harness the power of Crouching Tigers with the Mystic Ninja; Zen, Tamer of Purpose
Ward off threats with the Mystic Illusionist; Enigma, Ledger of Ancestry
Part the Mistveil booster set contains a total of 239* cards, with the following configuration and estimated rarity breakdown:

1 Fabled
6 Legendary*
43 Majestic (1 per 4 packs)
54 Rare (1.83 per pack)
123 Common (11 per pack)
12 Token (1.84 per pack)
Premium Foil (1 per pack)
1 Fabled (1 per ??? packs)
6 Legendary (1 per 96 packs)
32 Majestic (1 per 18 packs)
45 Rare (5 per 24 packs)
86 Common (18 per 24 packs)
28 Cold Foil (1 per 24 packs)
1 Fabled
5 Legendary
5 Majestic
3 Rare
14 Common
18* Marvels (1 per 100 packs)
13 Majestics are Expansion content to support hero’s and classes that are not featured in the core product.

*Japanese language product has 1 additional Legendary and Marvel.

“Gold Pack”
A special 3-card “Gold Pack” can be found in approximately 1 in 20 Part the Mistveil booster displays. It is a 25th pack in a display. It features in all 6 localized language products.

Japanese and French products have their own localized “Gold Pack”.

Spanish, Italian and German products have an English “Gold Pack”.


Each hero featured in Part the Mistveil also has their own Blitz deck. Each Blitz Deck contains a cohesive 40-card deck + hero card, weapon, equipment set, and tokens if required perfect for kitchen table gaming and learning how to play Flesh and Blood!

Print Run	Date Printed	Printed In	Languages	Out of Print	Size of Print Run
Booster	February 2024	Belgium, Japan	EN / JP / DE / FR / IT / SP	Yes	TBA
Blitz Deck	From March 2024	Belgium, Japan	EN / JP	Yes	TBA

Home Collector’s Centre Rosetta
Rosetta
Rosetta is a core booster set. It is Flesh and Blood TCGs fourteenth booster set release.

Worldwide Release date: September 20, 2024
Languages: English, Japanese, German, French, Italian, and Spanish
Rosetta returns to the mythical sanctuary of Aria, through thorny thickets and volatile thunderstorms, deep into the dense undergrowth where the forces of Earth and Lightning converge!

With the return to Aria comes the return of the Elemental talent, that will see heroes wield and meld Earth and Lightning cards like never before!

Rosetta marks the first ever set featuring all ARCANE classes, introducing two new Wizards and two new Runeblades!

With a brand new two-class / two-talent set structure opening up new Sealed Deck and Booster Draft possibilities, the return of the Elemental talent to Constructed, and a collection of 24 stunning Full Art Marvel cards, Rosetta will enchant players and collectors alike.

Ride the Lightning with the Elemental Runeblade; Aurora, Shooting Star
Use the wisdom of the Aetherscribes to protect the future with the Elemental Wizard; Oscilio, Constella Intelligence
Embrace the cycle of life with the Elemental Runeblade; Florian, Rotwood Harbinger
Feel the Heartbeat of Candlehold with the Elemental Wizard; Verdance, Thorn of the Rose
Rosetta booster set contains a total of 258* cards, with the following configuration and estimated rarity breakdown:

1 Fabled
5 Legendary*
49 Majestic (1 per 4 packs)
57 Rare (1.83 per pack)
128 Common (11 per pack)
14 Token (1.54 per pack)
36 Puzzle (6 per 24 packs)
Premium Foil (1 per pack)
1 Fabled (1 per ??? packs)
5 Legendary (1 per 96 packs)
40 Majestic (1 per 18 packs)
52 Rare (5 per 24 packs)
81 Common (18 per 24 packs)
28 Cold Foil (1 per 24 packs)
1 Fabled
5 Legendary
8 Majestic
5 Token
11 Common
24* Marvels
15 Majestics are Expansion content to support hero’s and classes that are not featured in the core product.

*Japanese language product has 2 additional Legendary cards; Arcanite Skullcap and Shock Charmers.

Each hero featured in Rosetta also has their own Blitz deck. Each Blitz Deck contains a cohesive 40-card deck + hero card, weapon, equipment set, and tokens if required perfect for kitchen table gaming and learning how to play Flesh and Blood!

Print Run	Date Printed	Printed In	Languages	Out of Print	Size of Print Run
Booster	From July 2024	Belgium, Japan	EN / JP / DE / FR / IT / SP	Yes	TBA
Blitz Deck	From July 2024	Belgium, Japan	EN / JP	Yes	TBA

Home Collector’s Centre The Hunted
The Hunted
The Hunted is a core booster set. It is Flesh and Blood TCGs fifteenth booster set release.

Worldwide Release date: January 31, 2025
Languages: English, Japanese, German, French, Italian, and Spanish
The Hunted calls players to take up the mantle of two vengeful Dracai – high ranking officers in the loyalist army. With their Emperor slain, they ride out across the fiery plains of Volcor to bring the killers to justice.

The Hunted features heroes from the Ninja, Warrior, and Assassin classes, exceptional Sealed Deck and Booster Draft play with lots and lots of stabbing, and a collection of breathtaking Marvels unlike anything you’ve ever seen!

Heroes;

Royal Draconic Ninja; Cindra, Dracai of Retribution
Royal Draconic Warrior; Fang, Dracai of Blades
Chaos Assassin; Arakni, Marionette
The Hunted booster set contains a total of 264* cards, with the following configuration and estimated rarity breakdown:

1 Fabled
6 Legendary**
42 Majestic* (1 per 4 packs)
66 Rare (1.83 per pack)
130 Common (11 per pack)
16 Token (1.54 per pack)
Premium Foil (1 per pack)
1 Fabled (1 per ??? packs)
6 Legendary (1 per 96 packs)
33 Majestic (1 per 18 packs)
60 Rare (5 per 24 packs)
107 Common (18 per 24 packs)
33 Cold Foil (1 per 24 packs)
1 Fabled
5 Legendary
7 Majestic
4 Rare
16 Common
17 Marvels

*15 Majestics are Expansion content to support hero’s and classes that are not featured in the core product.

**Japanese language product has 2 additional Legendary cards; Braveforge Bracers and Valiant Dynamo.

Each hero featured in The Hunted also has their own Blitz deck, including an original version of Arakni! Each Blitz Deck contains a cohesive 40-card deck + hero card, weapon, equipment set, and tokens if required perfect for kitchen table gaming and learning how to play Flesh and Blood!

Print Run	Date Printed	Printed In	Languages	Out of Print	Size of Print Run
Booster	From November 2024	Belgium, Japan	EN / JP / DE / FR / IT / SP	Yes	TBA
Blitz Deck Collection	From November 2024	Belgium	EN	Yes	TBA

Collector's Centre
High Seas
High Seas
High Seas is a core booster set. It is Flesh and Blood TCGs sixteenth booster set release.

Worldwide Release date: June 6, 2025
Languages: English, Japanese, French
Set sail for the High Seas in search of ancient treasure, big game sea monsters, and the adventure of a lifetime!

High Seas introduces the highly anticipated Pirate and Necromancer classes to Flesh and Blood. Three new dual-class heroes will navigate Rathe's treacherous open waters, each wielding a unique swashbuckling strategy that taps into previously uncharted waters of Flesh and Blood game design!

Gravy Bones, Shipwrecked Looter
Puffin, Hightail
Marlynn, Treasure Hunter
“Ye ain't a proper Pirate unless ye've got a taste for salt and a hunger for treasure!”

Discover breathtaking Marvels, Pirate Booty, and Lost Treasures thought to exist only in fables and folklore, in Treasure Packs found in each display of High Seas!

All hands on decks! It's time to set sail for the High Seas!

High Seas booster set contains a total of 265 cards, with the following configuration and estimated rarity breakdown:

1 Fabled
6 Legendary
46 Majestic (1 per 4 packs)
64 Rare (1.83 per pack)
127 Common (11 per pack)
18 Basic
Premium Foil (1 per pack)
1 Fabled (1 per ??? packs)
6 Legendary (1 per 96 packs)
33 Majestic (1 per 18 packs)
60 Rare (5 per 24 packs)
85 Common (18 per 24 packs)
21 Marvels (1 per 60 packs)

Stated card drop frequencies are an approximate average across the entire production of a product, and are not guaranteed to exist in any given pack, display, or case of product. Due to variations that may occur in the manufacturing process, final distributions of cards may differ from those stated above.

Treasure Pack
Treasure Packs are found atop each display of High Seas! Discover breathtaking marvels, pirate booty, and lost treasures - thought to exist on in fables and folklore!

High Seas Treasure Pack set contains a total of 90 cards, with the following configuration and estimated rarity breakdown:

11 Marvel
4 Legendary
52 Pirate Booty
14 Common
9 Puzzle Pieces
1 Treasure Pack per display*
3 cards per pack
1 Gold Slot (Double-sided Rainbow Foil)
1 Treasure Slot*
1 Map Slot
43 different Lost Treasures to discover (in addition to the 90 card set)

17 unique Lost Treasure (only 1 of each exist in Treasure Packs)

Lost Treasure appears 1:1,000 Treasure Packs

*Treasure Slot contains a Cold Foil or a Lost Treasure

Home Collector’s Centre Super Slam
Super Slam
Super Slam is a core booster set. It is Flesh and Blood TCG’s 17th booster set release.

Worldwide Release date: September 26, 2025
Languages: English, French, Japanese
Super Slam pits Guardians and Brutes against each other in the Deathmatch Arena with no weapons – just fists and wits. Revered heroes draw on the crowd’s respect, while Reviled heroes play dirty! Whichever side you choose, it’ll be the show of a lifetime!

Tuffnut, Bumbling Hulkster
Pleiades, Superstar
Kayo, Underhanded Cheat
Lyath Goldmane, Vile Savant
Super Slam booster set contains a total of 276 cards, with the following configuration and estimated rarity breakdown:

1 Fabled
5 Legendary
42 Majestic
14 Set (1 per 8 packs)
24 Expansion (1 per 6 packs)
40 Super Rare (1 per 2.18 packs)
40 Rare (1.42 per pack)
134 Common (11 per pack)
14 Basic
1 Premium Foil (1 per pack)
1 Fabled (1 per ??? packs)
5 Legendary (1 per 94 packs)
21 Majestic (1 per 22 packs)
36 Super Rare (1 per 13 packs)
39 Rare (4 per 24 packs)
111 Common (17 per 24 packs)
47 Cold Foil (1 per 24 packs)
1 Fabled
14 Marvel
5 Legendary
13 Majestic
1 Rare
13 Common
Stated card drop frequencies are an approximate average across the entire production of a product, and are not guaranteed to exist in any given pack, display, or case of product. Due to variations that may occur in the manufacturing process, final distributions of cards may differ from those stated above.

Home Collector’s Centre Gold Foil Prize Cards
Gold Foil Prize Cards
The following tables group the Gold Foils by the programs that award them, so an effective “Drop Rate” can be displayed. For example, ProQuest awards a Black Envelop to the winner which can contain a Gold Foil Majestic, Rare, or Common, which is why these cards are grouped together to create a “Drop Rate” from within this pool.

The current programs that award Gold Foils are:

Type of Gold Foil	Available At
Gold Foil Legendary	World Championship
Pro Tour
Calling
National Championship (dependent on size of event)
Gold Foil Majestic, Rare, Common	Pro Quest
Showdown
Battlegrounds
Other selected programs
